 In modern life, most of us fall asleep without eating at night after a day of work pressure and fatigue
 vahiin kuch log motaape ke dar se raat main khaanaa nahin khate hai
 But the habit of sleeping without eating anything can severely damage health
 vahiin, khaali pet sone se kai bimariyon kaa khatra bhi bad jaataa he
 Let's know how sleeping on empty stomach causes harm to the body
 1
 Lack of energy - Many people feel that the body does not need to eat at night
 lekin health export ke mutabik, sharir 24 ghante energy produs karata he or har samay calories bern karne kaa kaam karata he
 For this, the body needs nutrients
 florida state uniwarsity ke shodhakartaaon ke mutabik, jo purush raat ko sone se pehle protein shaike kaa seven karte hai wo duusare logon ke mukaable zyada energetic mahasoos karte hai
 Likewise, sleeping on an empty stomach at night can lead to fatigue the next day, affecting your ability to work
 2
 Metabolism affects - Metabolism is affected by people who have a habit of sleeping without eating dinner
 isse sharir kaa insulin level bhi prabhavit hota he
 Apart from this, sleeping on an empty stomach also worsens cholesterol and thyroid levels
 yah aadat kai bimariyon kaa shikaar bana sakati he
 3
 sone main dikkat-khaali pet sone se der raat bhukh kii vajah se pet dard ho saktaa he, jisase aapaki neend bhi distorb ho sakati he
 So if you want to have a restful sleep, do not sleep without eating
 4
 Weight gain - Many people suffering from obesity feel that sleeping on an empty stomach at night reduces weight quickly
 aapako bhi agar aisa lagata he to aap galat hai
 However, health experts recommend eating light food at night
 lekin bina khaae sona sehat ko nuksaan pahunchane ke saath vajan bhi badhaata he
 5
 sharir main neutrishan kii kami-raat ke samay bhukhe pet sone se sharir main nutrishan kii kami ho jaati he
 According to health experts, the body needs many nutrients to stay healthy
 lekin raat ko khaali pet sone se vyakti ke sharir main in sabhi nutrients kii kami ho jaati he, jo unhen kai bimariyon kaa shikaar bana sakati he
